Abstraction for an S\+DR tranceiver device -\/ configuration and streaming.

\paragraph[{acquire\+Read\+Buffer(\+Stream $\ast$stream, size\+\_\+t \&handle, const void $\ast$$\ast$buffs, int \&flags, long long \&time\+Ns, const long timeout\+Us=100000)}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf int} Soapy\+S\+D\+R.\+Device\+::acquire\+Read\+Buffer (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Stream $\ast$}]{stream, }
\item[{size\+\_\+t \&}]{handle, }
\item[{const {\bf void} $\ast$$\ast$}]{buffs, }
\item[{{\bf int} \&}]{flags, }
\item[{long long \&}]{time\+Ns, }
\item[{const long}]{timeout\+Us = {\ttfamily 100000}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a5b7e6de66fa521a44221f46146ae6fac}
Acquire direct buffers from a receive stream. This call is part of the direct buffer access A\+PI.

The buffs array will be filled with a stream pointer for each channel. Each pointer can be read up to the number of return value elements.

The handle will be set by the implementation so that the caller may later release access to the buffers with \doxyref{release\+Read\+Buffer()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a089ce8e867ca832db9b3e62085753cd9}. Handle represents an index into the internal scatter/gather table such that handle is between 0 and num direct buffers -\/ 1.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
{\em handle} & an index value used in the release() call \\
\hline
{\em buffs} & an array of void$\ast$ buffers num chans in size \\
\hline
{\em flags} & optional flag indicators about the result \\
\hline
{\em time\+Ns} & the buffer\textquotesingle{}s timestamp in nanoseconds \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Us} & the timeout in microseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of elements read per buffer or error code 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Acquire direct buffers from a transmit stream. This call is part of the direct buffer access A\+PI.

The buffs array will be filled with a stream pointer for each channel. Each pointer can be written up to the number of return value elements.

The handle will be set by the implementation so that the caller may later release access to the buffers with \doxyref{release\+Write\+Buffer()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a63e6f572357d24edafb609422a5c9354}. Handle represents an index into the internal scatter/gather table such that handle is between 0 and num direct buffers -\/ 1.

\index{Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device@{Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device}!activate\+Stream@{activate\+Stream}}

\paragraph[{activate\+Stream(\+Stream $\ast$stream, const int flags=0, const long long time\+Ns=0, const size\+\_\+t num\+Elems=0)}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf int} Soapy\+S\+D\+R.\+Device\+::activate\+Stream (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Stream $\ast$}]{stream, }
\item[{const {\bf int}}]{flags = {\ttfamily 0}, }
\item[{const long long}]{time\+Ns = {\ttfamily 0}, }

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a9acf785fb3ae8bfa1b00ac5fbd61e373}
Activate a stream. Call activate to prepare a stream before using read/write(). The implementation control switches or stimulate data flow.

The time\+Ns is only valid when the flags have S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+H\+A\+S\+\_\+\+T\+I\+ME. The num\+Elems count can be used to request a finite burst size. The S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+E\+N\+D\+\_\+\+B\+U\+R\+ST flag can signal end on the finite burst. Not all implementations will support the full range of options. In this case, the implementation returns S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
{\em flags} & optional flag indicators about the stream \\
\hline
{\em time\+Ns} & optional activation time in nanoseconds \\
\hline
{\em num\+Elems} & optional element count for burst control \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 for success or error code on failure 
\end{DoxyReturn}

)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a1002640ce095095dc44b3ecc258f895c}
Get the buffer addresses for a scatter/gather table entry. When the underlying D\+MA implementation uses scatter/gather then this call provides the user addresses for that table.

Example\+: The caller may query the D\+MA memory addresses once after stream creation to pre-\/allocate a re-\/usable ring-\/buffer.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
{\em handle} & an index value between 0 and num direct buffers -\/ 1 \\
\hline
{\em buffs} & an array of void$\ast$ buffers num chans in size \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 for success or error code when not supported 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a1e27b9e8a89fe20f27483b090c308751}
Get the stream\textquotesingle{}s maximum transmission unit (M\+TU) in number of elements. The M\+TU specifies the maximum payload transfer in a stream operation. This value can be used as a stream buffer allocation size that can best optimize throughput given the underlying stream implementation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the M\+TU in number of stream elements (never zero) 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\paragraph[{read\+Stream(\+Stream $\ast$stream, void $\ast$const $\ast$buffs, const size\+\_\+t num\+Elems, int \&flags, long long \&time\+Ns, const long timeout\+Us=100000)}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf int} Soapy\+S\+D\+R.\+Device\+::read\+Stream (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{Stream $\ast$}]{stream, }
\item[{{\bf void} $\ast$const $\ast$}]{buffs, }

Read elements from a stream for reception. This is a multi-\/channel call, and buffs should be an array of void $\ast$, where each pointer will be filled with data from a different channel.

{\bfseries Client code compatibility\+:} The \doxyref{read\+Stream()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a89de55a8e441182f377870fe2cf6f32f} call should be well defined at all times, including prior to activation and after deactivation. When inactive, \doxyref{read\+Stream()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a89de55a8e441182f377870fe2cf6f32f} should implement the timeout specified by the caller and return S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+O\+UT.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
{\em buffs} & an array of void$\ast$ buffers num chans in size \\
\hline
{\em num\+Elems} & the number of elements in each buffer \\
\hline
{\em flags} & optional flag indicators about the result \\
\hline
{\em time\+Ns} & the buffer\textquotesingle{}s timestamp in nanoseconds \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Us} & the timeout in microseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of elements read per buffer or error code 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line {\bf 106} of file {\bf Device.\+cpp}.

\paragraph[{read\+Stream\+Status(\+Stream $\ast$stream, size\+\_\+t \&chan\+Mask, int \&flags, long long \&time\+Ns, const long timeout\+Us=100000)}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf int} Soapy\+S\+D\+R.\+Device\+::read\+Stream\+Status (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a1487c704c3b8492c7d8374017fa48020}
Readback status information about a stream. This call is typically used on a transmit stream to report time errors, underflows, and burst completion.

{\bfseries Client code compatibility\+:} Client code may continually poll \doxyref{read\+Stream\+Status()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_abb2b3e209ca22209f922d8aadfc78338} in a loop. Implementations of \doxyref{read\+Stream\+Status()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_abb2b3e209ca22209f922d8aadfc78338} should wait in the call for a status change event or until the timeout expiration. When stream status is not implemented on a particular stream, \doxyref{read\+Stream\+Status()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_abb2b3e209ca22209f922d8aadfc78338} should return S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED. Client code may use this indication to disable a polling loop.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
{\em chan\+Mask} & to which channels this status applies \\
\hline
{\em flags} & optional input flags and output flags \\
\hline
{\em time\+Ns} & the buffer\textquotesingle{}s timestamp in nanoseconds \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Us} & the timeout in microseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 for success or error code like timeout 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line {\bf 116} of file {\bf Device.\+cpp}.

Release an acquired buffer back to the transmit stream. This call is part of the direct buffer access A\+PI.

Stream meta-\/data is provided as part of the release call, and not the acquire call so that the caller may acquire buffers without committing to the contents of the meta-\/data, which can be determined by the user as the buffers are filled.

\index{set\+Frequency@{set\+Frequency}!Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device@{Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device}}
\paragraph[{set\+Frequency(const int direction, const size\+\_\+t channel, const double frequency, const Kwargs \&args=\+Kwargs())}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf void} Soapy\+S\+D\+R.\+Device\+::set\+Frequency (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const {\bf int}}]{direction, }
\item[{const size\+\_\+t}]{channel, }
\item[{const double}]{frequency, }
\item[{const {\bf Kwargs} \&}]{args = {\ttfamily {\bf Kwargs}()}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a62e294e21bf2f11512c1c941aa270fe8}
Set the center frequency of the chain.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For RX, this specifies the down-\/conversion frequency.
\item For TX, this specifies the up-\/conversion frequency.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The default implementation of \doxyref{set\+Frequency()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a63fbf5fc9b091053888e5fa707fbedac} will tune the \char`\"{}\+R\+F\char`\"{} component as close as possible to the requested center frequency. Tuning inaccuracies will be compensated for with the \char`\"{}\+B\+B\char`\"{} component.

The args can be used to augment the tuning algorithm.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Use \char`\"{}\+O\+F\+F\+S\+E\+T\char`\"{} to specify an \char`\"{}\+R\+F\char`\"{} tuning offset, usually with the intention of moving the LO out of the passband. The offset will be compensated for using the \char`\"{}\+B\+B\char`\"{} component.
\item Use the name of a component for the key and a frequency in Hz as the value (any format) to enforce a specific frequency. The other components will be tuned with compensation to achieve the specified overall frequency.
\item Use the name of a component for the key and the value \char`\"{}\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\char`\"{} so that the tuning algorithm will avoid altering the component.
\item Vendor specific implementations can also use the same args to augment tuning in other ways such as specifying fractional vs integer N tuning.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em direction} & the channel direction RX or TX \\
\hline
{\em channel} & an available channel on the device \\
\hline
{\em frequency} & the center frequency in Hz \\
\hline
{\em args} & optional tuner arguments \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Definition at line {\bf 340} of file {\bf Device.\+cpp}.

Tune the center frequency of the specified element.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For RX, this specifies the down-\/conversion frequency.
\item For TX, this specifies the up-\/conversion frequency.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Recommended names used to represent tunable components\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}\+C\+O\+R\+R\char`\"{} -\/ freq error correction in P\+PM
\item \char`\"{}\+R\+F\char`\"{} -\/ frequency of the RF frontend
\item \char`\"{}\+B\+B\char`\"{} -\/ frequency of the baseband D\+SP
\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device@{Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device}!setup\+Stream@{setup\+Stream}}
\index{setup\+Stream@{setup\+Stream}!Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device@{Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Device}}
\paragraph[{setup\+Stream(const int direction, const std\+::string \&format, const std\+::vector$<$ size\+\_\+t $>$ \&channels=std\+::vector$<$ size\+\_\+t $>$(), const Kwargs \&args=\+Kwargs())}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Soapy\+S\+D\+R\+::\+Stream $\ast$ Soapy\+S\+D\+R.\+Device\+::setup\+Stream (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const {\bf int}}]{direction, }
\item[{const {\bf std\+::string} \&}]{format, }
\item[{const {\bf std\+::vector}$<$ size\+\_\+t $>$ \&}]{channels = {\ttfamily {\bf std\+::vector}$<$size\+\_\+t$>$()}, }
\item[{const {\bf Kwargs} \&}]{args = {\ttfamily {\bf Kwargs}()}}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\label{classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a122997121bbd82c67e77a9f9c86a8824}
Initialize a stream given a list of channels and stream arguments. The implementation may change switches or power-\/up components. All stream A\+PI calls should be usable with the new stream object after \doxyref{setup\+Stream()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a539c389e8b1d33dbccec524e5771461a} is complete, regardless of the activity state.

The A\+PI allows any number of simultaneous TX and RX streams, but many dual-\/channel devices are limited to one stream in each direction, using either one or both channels. This call will throw an exception if an unsupported combination is requested, or if a requested channel in this direction is already in use by another stream.

When multiple channels are added to a stream, they are typically expected to have the same sample rate. See \doxyref{set\+Sample\+Rate()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_a58514263b37e11f7229e24d5376a55a1}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em direction} & the channel direction ({\ttfamily S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+RX} or {\ttfamily S\+O\+A\+P\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+D\+R\+\_\+\+TX}) \\
\hline
{\em format} & A string representing the desired buffer format in read/write\+Stream() 

The first character selects the number type\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}\+C\char`\"{} means complex
\item \char`\"{}\+F\char`\"{} means floating point
\item \char`\"{}\+S\char`\"{} means signed integer
\item \char`\"{}\+U\char`\"{} means unsigned integer
\end{DoxyItemize}

The type character is followed by the number of bits per number (complex is 2x this size per sample)

Example format strings\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}\+C\+F32\char`\"{} -\/ complex float32 (8 bytes per element)
\item \char`\"{}\+C\+S16\char`\"{} -\/ complex int16 (4 bytes per element)
\item \char`\"{}\+C\+S12\char`\"{} -\/ complex int12 (3 bytes per element)
\item \char`\"{}\+C\+S4\char`\"{} -\/ complex int4 (1 byte per element)
\item \char`\"{}\+S32\char`\"{} -\/ int32 (4 bytes per element)
\item \char`\"{}\+U8\char`\"{} -\/ uint8 (1 byte per element)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\\
\hline
{\em channels} & a list of channels or empty for automatic. \\
\hline
{\em args} & stream args or empty for defaults. 

Recommended keys to use in the args dictionary\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \char`\"{}\+W\+I\+R\+E\char`\"{} -\/ format of the samples between device and host 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an opaque pointer to a stream handle. 

The returned stream is not required to have internal locking, and may not be used concurrently from multiple threads. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Definition at line {\bf 80} of file {\bf Device.\+cpp}.

Perform a S\+PI transaction and return the result. Its up to the implementation to set the clock rate, and read edge, and the write edge of the S\+PI core. S\+PI slaves without a readback pin will return 0.

If the device contains multiple S\+PI masters, the address bits can encode which master.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

the readback data, num\+Bits-\/1 is first in

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

Write elements to a stream for transmission. This is a multi-\/channel call, and buffs should be an array of void $\ast$, where each pointer will be filled with data for a different channel.

{\bfseries Client code compatibility\+:} Client code relies on \doxyref{write\+Stream()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_add0352143b02e553ef234670828ca7c9} for proper back-\/pressure. The \doxyref{write\+Stream()}{p.}{dd/de0/classSoapySDR_1_1Device_add0352143b02e553ef234670828ca7c9} implementation must enforce the timeout such that the call blocks until space becomes available or timeout expiration.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream} & the opaque pointer to a stream handle \\
\hline
{\em buffs} & an array of void$\ast$ buffers num chans in size \\
\hline
{\em num\+Elems} & the number of elements in each buffer \\
\hline
{\em flags} & optional input flags and output flags \\
\hline
{\em time\+Ns} & the buffer\textquotesingle{}s timestamp in nanoseconds \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+Us} & the timeout in microseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of elements written per buffer or error 
\end{DoxyReturn}
